Moved those four imports inside `build_app()` (the function is only called after `plan_launch()` confirms the dependency probe is clean), kept the stdlib-only submodules (`audit`, `state`, `setup`, `auth.token_store`, `graph.registry`) at module top, and added four new tests in `tests/test_m365_runtime_0_1_2_readiness_fix.py`: (1) `test_launcher_imports_when_httpx_absent_at_import_time` spawns a Python subprocess that poisons `sys.modules['httpx']=None` BEFORE importing the launcher and asserts the module imports cleanly and `plan_launch().outcome == 'dependency_missing'` with `'httpx'` in `missing_modules`; (2) the same proof for `fastapi`; (3) the same proof for `uvicorn`; (4) `test_launcher_top_level_does_not_import_dependency_sensitive_submodules` is a static guard that scans the launcher source and fails on any forbidden top-level import line.
